        network 500 create
            description "for marking"
            ingress
                default-action fc be profile in
                dscp be fc be profile in
                dscp cs1 fc l2 profile in
                dscp cs2 fc l2 profile in
                dscp cs3 fc l2 profile in
                dscp cs4 fc h1 profile in
                dscp cs5 fc af profile in
                dscp nc1 fc nc profile in
                dscp nc2 fc af profile in
                lsp-exp 0 fc be profile in
                lsp-exp 1 fc l2 profile in
                lsp-exp 2 fc l2 profile in
                lsp-exp 3 fc l2 profile in
                lsp-exp 4 fc h1 profile in
                lsp-exp 5 fc af profile in
                lsp-exp 6 fc nc profile in
                lsp-exp 7 fc af profile in
            exit
            egress
                remarking
                fc af
                    dscp-in-profile cs5
                    dscp-out-profile cs5
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 5
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 5
                exit
                fc h1
                    dscp-in-profile cs4
                    dscp-out-profile cs4
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 4
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 4
                exit
                fc nc
                    dscp-in-profile nc1
                    dscp-out-profile nc1
                    lsp-exp-in-profile 6
                    lsp-exp-out-profile 6
                exit
            exit
        exit
    exit

                        match
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 601
                        match
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 608
                        match
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 609
                        match
                            router Base
                        exit

                        match
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                exit
                mac-filter
                    no shutdown
                exit
            exit
        exit

#--------------------------------------------------
    router Base

echo "ISIS Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
        isis 0
            no shutdown
        exit

echo "PIM Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
        pim
            no shutdown
        exit
#--------------------------------------------------
echo "Policy Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
        policy-options
            begin
            prefix-list "system1"
                prefix 0.0.0.0/0 prefix-length-range 32-32
            exit
            prefix-list "plDefaultRoute"
                prefix 0.0.0.0/0 exact
            exit
            prefix-list "plPrivateRoute "
                prefix 10.0.0.0/8 prefix-length-range 24-32
                prefix 172.16.0.0/12 longer
                prefix 192.168.0.0/16 longer
            exit
            community "JH-EPON" members "target:64759:10001100"
            community "JH-GPON" members "target:64759:20909000"
            community "cmJHMAN" members "64759:1503" "64759:46013"
            community "64759:10" members "target:64759:10"
            community "64759:11" members "target:64759:11"
            policy-statement "label-filter"
                entry 10
                    from
                        prefix-list "system1"
                    exit
                    action accept
                    exit
                exit
                entry 20
                    action reject
                exit
            exit
            policy-statement "JH-EPON-export"
                entry 10
                    action accept
                        community add "JH-EPON"
                    exit
                exit
            exit
            policy-statement "JH-GPON-export"
                entry 10
                    action accept
                        community add "JH-GPON"
                    exit
                exit
            exit
            policy-statement "rpSET_COMM_OUT"
                entry 10
                    from
                        prefix-list "plDefaultRoute"
                    exit
                    to
                        protocol bgp
                    exit
                    action reject
                exit
                entry 20
                    from
                        prefix-list "plPrivateRoute "
                    exit
                    to
                        protocol bgp
                    exit
                    action reject
                exit
                entry 30
                    from
                        protocol direct
                    exit
                    to
                        protocol bgp
                    exit
                    action accept
                        community replace "cmJHMAN"
                    exit
                exit
                entry 40
                    from
                        protocol static
                        tag 100
                    exit
                    to
                        protocol bgp
                    exit
                    action accept
                        community replace "cmJHMAN"
                    exit
                exit
            exit
            policy-statement "rpStaticToISIS"
                entry 10
                    from
                        protocol static
                        tag 10
                    exit
                    to
                        protocol isis
                    exit
                    action accept
                    exit
                exit
            exit
            policy-statement "JH-EPON&GPON-import"
                entry 10
                    from
                        protocol bgp-vpn
                        community "JH-GPON"
                    exit
                    action accept
                    exit
                exit
                entry 20
                    from
                        protocol bgp-vpn
                        community "JH-EPON"
                    exit
                    action accept
                    exit
                exit
            exit
            policy-statement "export-direct-to-ospf"
                entry 10
                    from
                        protocol direct
                    exit
                    to
                        protocol ospf
                    exit
                    action accept
                        metric set 10
                        type 1
                    exit
                exit
                entry 20
                    from
                        protocol static
                    exit
                    to
                        protocol ospf
                    exit
                    action accept
                    exit
                exit
            exit
            policy-statement "export-static-to-ospf"
                entry 10
                    from
                        protocol static
                        prefix-list "static-to-ospf"
                    exit
                    to
                        protocol ospf
                    exit
                    action accept
                    exit
                exit
            exit
            policy-statement "target:64759:11_import"
                description "device"
                entry 10
                    from
                        protocol bgp-vpn
                        community "64759:11"
                    exit
                    action accept
                    exit
                exit
                entry 20
                    from
                        protocol bgp-vpn
                        community "64759:10"
                    exit
                    action accept
                    exit
                exit
            exit
            commit
        exit

echo "BGP Configuration"

        bgp
            multipath 8
